   Meaning: A period of isolation imposed to prevent the spread of disease.
   Example: "The ship was placed in quarantine due to a suspected outbreak."

292. AILMENT
   Phonetic: /ˈeɪlmənt/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A minor illness.
   Example: "He suffered from a minor ailment after returning from his trip."

293. DIAGNOSIS
   Phonetic: /ˌdaɪəɡˈnəʊsɪs/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: The identification of the nature of an illness or other problem by examination of the symptoms.
   Example: "The doctor made a diagnosis after reviewing the test results."

294. MEDICATION
   Phonetic: /ˌmedɪˈkeɪʃən/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A substance used for medical treatment, especially a medicine.
   Example: "She takes medication daily to manage her condition."

295. INCIDENCE
   Phonetic: /ˈɪnsɪdəns/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: The occurrence, rate, or frequency of a disease, crime, or other undesirable thing.
   Example: "The incidence of malaria is high in tropical regions."

296. PANDEMIC
   Phonetic: /pænˈdemɪk/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A disease prevalent over a whole country or the world.
   Example: "The COVID-19 pandemic affected global travel."

297. OUTBREAK
   Phonetic: /ˈaʊtbreɪk/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A sudden occurrence of something unwelcome, such as war or disease.
   Example: "An outbreak of food poisoning occurred at the hotel."

298. MORTALITY
   Phonetic: /mɔːrˈtæləti/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: The state of being subject to death; also the rate of death.
   Example: "The mortality rate was reduced due to improved healthcare."

299. EPIDEMIC
   Phonetic: /ˌepɪˈdemɪk/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A widespread occurrence of an infectious disease in a community at a particular time.
   Example: "The city experienced an epidemic of the flu."

300. IMMUNE
   Phonetic: /ɪˈmjuːn/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: Protected against a particular disease.
   Example: "He is immune to chickenpox because he had it as a child."

301. TRANSMIT
   Phonetic: /trænzˈmɪt/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: To pass something on to someone else.
   Example: "Mosquitoes can transmit diseases like malaria."

302. CONTAMINATED
   Phonetic: /kənˈtæmɪneɪtɪd/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: Made impure by exposure to or addition of a poisonous or polluting substance.
   Example: "The water supply was contaminated with bacteria."

303. INFECTIOUS
   Phonetic: /ɪnˈfekʃəs/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: Likely to be transmitted to people through the environment.
   Example: "The flu is highly infectious, so stay home if you're sick."

304. PREVENTION
   Phonetic: /prɪˈvenʃən/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: The action of stopping something from happening or arising.
   Example: "Disease prevention is better than cure."

305. IMMUNIZATION
   Phonetic: /ˌɪmjunɪˈzeɪʃən/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: The process of making a person or animal immune to infection by vaccination.
   Example: "Immunization programs have eradicated many diseases."

306. SYMPTOM
   Phonetic: /ˈsɪmptəm/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A physical or mental feature which is regarded as indicating a condition of disease.
   Example: "A common symptom of the flu is a high fever."

307. TREATMENT
   Phonetic: /ˈtriːtmənt/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: Medical care given to a patient for an illness or injury.
   Example: "He received treatment for his injuries at the hospital."

308. CHRONIC
   Phonetic: /ˈkrɑːnɪk/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: Persisting for a long time or constantly recurring.
   Example: "She suffers from a chronic back pain."

309. ALTITUDE
   Phonetic: /ˈæltɪtjuːd/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: The height of an object or point in relation to sea level or ground level.
   Example: "At high altitude, it's harder to breathe."

310. ALTITUDE SICKNESS
   Phonetic: /ˈæltɪtjuːd ˈsɪknəs/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: Illness caused by ascending too high too quickly without acclimatization.
   Example: "Some hikers experience altitude sickness when climbing mountains."

311. HYPOTHERMIA
   Phonetic: /ˌhaɪpəˈθɜːrmiə/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: The condition of having an abnormally low body temperature.
   Example: "Exposure to cold weather can lead to hypothermia."

312. DEHYDRATION
   Phonetic: /ˌdiːhaɪˈdreɪʃən/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A harmful reduction in the amount of water in the body.
   Example: "Drink plenty of water to avoid dehydration, especially in hot weather."

313. BURN
   Phonetic: /bɜːrn/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: An injury caused by heat, electricity, radiation, or chemicals.
   Example: "She suffered a severe burn while cooking."

314. FRACTURE

   Meaning: A crack or break in a bone.
   Example: "He sustained a leg fracture during the accident."

   Example: "The snake's venom is deadly."

   Phonetic: /ˈæntɪdəʊt/

   Phonetic: /ˈswelɪŋ/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: An abnormal enlargement of a part of the body, typically as a result of inflammation or fluid retention.
   Example: "Apply ice to reduce the swelling."

319. INFLAMMATION
   Phonetic: /ˌɪnfləˈmeɪʃən/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A localized physical condition in which part of the body becomes reddened, swollen, hot, and often painful, especially as a reaction to injury or infection.
   Example: "Anti-inflammatory drugs can help reduce the inflammation."

320. COMPRESS
   Phonetic: /ˈkɑːm प्रेस/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A pad of cloth or absorbent material pressed onto a part of the body to relieve inflammation or stop bleeding.
   Example: "Apply a cold compress to reduce the swelling."

321. BANDAGE
   Phonetic: /ˈbændɪdʒ/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: A strip of woven material used to bind up a wound or protect an injured part of the body.

322. RESUSCITATION
   Phonetic: /rɪˌsʌsɪˈteɪʃən/

   Meaning: The action or process of reviving someone from unconsciousness or apparent death.
   Example: "The paramedics performed resuscitation on the victim."

323. CPR
   Phonetic: /ˌsiː piː ˈɑːr/
   Difficulty: intermediate
   Meaning: Cardiopulmonary resuscitation, a procedure to revive someone whose heart has stopped.

324. AIRWAY
   Phonetic: /ˈeərweɪ/
